Everyone wears masks, stands 6 feet away from their customers when talking to them, and closely monitors the store capacity (I even saw them gently ask someone to wait outside as he was just sitting in the store waiting for a friend/family to shop)!

The customer service is also top notch! I told Gant what I was looking for that day and he immediately took my budget into consideration while showing me their inventory. Not once did he try to up-sell me on anything. He gave me his opinion on every single item that I asked about, and even provided me a bunch of safety tips for being on the road since he knew I was just starting out!

There was a moment I was looking at an expensive item and Gant told me what was good about it, but also why it may not be necessary for me at this time. He then helped me find something better suited for my current needs (and it cost less, too!) He never made me feel pressured to buy any unnecessary gear. Gant didn't care that I didn't know anything about biking, he just wanted to make sure that when I got out onto the road, that I stayed safe no matter what!

Elmira is the best thing to happen to this stretch of McAllister Street for years (culinary or otherwise). We advised our server that we had a time limit for our meal and she not only served us quickly but got into the spirit of assisting us with our selection.
